-- public.flyway_schema_history definition

-- Drop table

-- DROP TABLE flyway_schema_history;

CREATE TABLE flyway_schema_history (
	installed_rank int4 NOT NULL,
	"version" varchar(50) NULL,
	description varchar(200) NOT NULL,
	"type" varchar(20) NOT NULL,
	script varchar(1000) NOT NULL,
	checksum int4 NULL,
	installed_by varchar(100) NOT NULL,
	installed_on timestamp DEFAULT now() NOT NULL,
	execution_time int4 NOT NULL,
	success bool NOT NULL,
	CONSTRAINT flyway_schema_history_pk PRIMARY KEY (installed_rank)
);
CREATE INDEX flyway_schema_history_s_idx ON public.flyway_schema_history USING btree (success);

-- public.lineage_events definition

-- Drop table

-- DROP TABLE lineage_events;

CREATE TABLE lineage_events (
	event_time timestamptz NOT NULL,
	"event" jsonb NOT NULL,
	event_type text NULL,
	job_name text NULL,
	job_namespace text NULL,
	producer text NULL,
	run_uuid uuid NULL,
	created_at timestamptz DEFAULT (now() AT TIME ZONE 'UTC'::text)::timestamp with time zone NULL,
	"_event_type" varchar(64) DEFAULT 'RUN_EVENT'::character varying NULL
);
CREATE INDEX lineage_events_created_at_index ON public.lineage_events USING btree (created_at DESC NULLS LAST);
CREATE INDEX lineage_events_event_time ON public.lineage_events USING btree (event_time DESC);

-- public.datasets definition

-- Drop table

-- DROP TABLE datasets;

CREATE TABLE datasets (
	"uuid" uuid NOT NULL,
	"type" varchar(64) NOT NULL,
	created_at timestamptz NOT NULL,
	updated_at timestamptz NOT NULL,
	namespace_uuid uuid NULL,
	source_uuid uuid NULL,
	"name" varchar NOT NULL,
	physical_name varchar NOT NULL,
	description text NULL,
	current_version_uuid uuid NULL,
	last_modified_at timestamp NULL,
	namespace_name varchar NULL,
	source_name varchar NULL,
	is_deleted bool DEFAULT false NULL,
	is_hidden bool DEFAULT false NULL,
	CONSTRAINT datasets_namespace_uuid_name_key UNIQUE (namespace_uuid, name),
	CONSTRAINT datasets_pkey PRIMARY KEY (uuid),
	CONSTRAINT datasets_namespace_uuid_fkey FOREIGN KEY (namespace_uuid) REFERENCES namespaces("uuid") ON DELETE CASCADE,
	CONSTRAINT datasets_source_uuid_fkey FOREIGN KEY (source_uuid) REFERENCES sources("uuid") ON DELETE CASCADE
);
CREATE UNIQUE INDEX dataset_name_index ON public.datasets USING btree (name, namespace_name);

-- Permissions

ALTER TABLE datasets OWNER TO marquez;
GRANT ALL ON TABLE datasets TO marquez;

-- public.jobs definition

-- Drop table

-- DROP TABLE jobs;

CREATE TABLE jobs (
	"uuid" uuid NOT NULL,
	"type" varchar(64) NOT NULL,
	created_at timestamptz NOT NULL,
	updated_at timestamptz NOT NULL,
	namespace_uuid uuid NULL,
	simple_name varchar NOT NULL,
	description text NULL,
	current_version_uuid uuid NULL,
	namespace_name varchar NULL,
	current_job_context_uuid uuid NULL,
	current_location varchar NULL,
	current_inputs jsonb NULL,
	symlink_target_uuid uuid NULL,
	parent_job_uuid uuid NULL,
	parent_job_uuid_string bpchar(36) DEFAULT ''::bpchar NULL,
	is_hidden bool DEFAULT false NULL,
	"name" varchar NOT NULL,
	aliases _varchar NULL,
	current_run_uuid uuid NULL,
	CONSTRAINT jobs_pkey PRIMARY KEY (uuid),
	CONSTRAINT unique_jobs_namespace_uuid_name_parent UNIQUE (namespace_uuid, name),
	CONSTRAINT jobs_namespace_uuid_fkey FOREIGN KEY (namespace_uuid) REFERENCES namespaces("uuid") ON DELETE CASCADE,
	CONSTRAINT jobs_parent_fk_jobs FOREIGN KEY (parent_job_uuid) REFERENCES jobs("uuid") ON DELETE CASCADE,
	CONSTRAINT jobs_symlink_target_uuid_fkey FOREIGN KEY (symlink_target_uuid) REFERENCES jobs("uuid") ON DELETE CASCADE
);
CREATE INDEX jobs_current_job_context_uuid_index ON public.jobs USING btree (current_job_context_uuid);
CREATE INDEX jobs_current_run_uuid_idx ON public.jobs USING btree (current_run_uuid);
CREATE INDEX jobs_current_version_uuid_index ON public.jobs USING btree (current_version_uuid) WHERE (current_version_uuid IS NOT NULL);
CREATE UNIQUE INDEX jobs_name_parent ON public.jobs USING btree (simple_name, namespace_name, parent_job_uuid);
CREATE INDEX jobs_symlink_target_uuid_index ON public.jobs USING btree (symlink_target_uuid) WHERE (symlink_target_uuid IS NOT NULL);
CREATE INDEX jobs_symlinks ON public.jobs USING btree (symlink_target_uuid) INCLUDE (uuid, namespace_name, simple_name) WHERE (symlink_target_uuid IS NOT NULL);

-- Permissions

ALTER TABLE jobs OWNER TO marquez;
GRANT ALL ON TABLE jobs TO marquez;

	"uuid" uuid NOT NULL,
	created_at timestamptz NOT NULL,
	dataset_uuid uuid NULL,
	"version" uuid NOT NULL,
	run_uuid uuid NULL,
	fields jsonb NULL,
	namespace_name varchar NULL,
	dataset_name varchar NULL,
	lifecycle_state varchar(63) NULL,
	dataset_schema_version_uuid uuid NULL,
	CONSTRAINT dataset_versions_dataset_uuid_version_key UNIQUE (dataset_uuid, version),
	CONSTRAINT dataset_versions_pkey PRIMARY KEY (uuid),
	CONSTRAINT dataset_versions_version UNIQUE (version),
	CONSTRAINT dataset_versions_dataset_schema_version_uuid_fkey FOREIGN KEY (dataset_schema_version_uuid) REFERENCES dataset_schema_versions("uuid"),
	CONSTRAINT dataset_versions_dataset_uuid_fkey FOREIGN KEY (dataset_uuid) REFERENCES datasets("uuid") ON DELETE CASCADE
);

	updated_at timestamp NOT NULL,

-- public.runs definition

-- Drop table

-- DROP TABLE runs;

CREATE TABLE runs (
	"uuid" uuid NOT NULL,
	created_at timestamptz NOT NULL,
	updated_at timestamptz NOT NULL,
	job_version_uuid uuid NULL,
	run_args_uuid uuid NULL,
	nominal_start_time timestamp NULL,
	nominal_end_time timestamp NULL,
	current_run_state varchar(64) NULL,
	start_run_state_uuid uuid NULL,
	end_run_state_uuid uuid NULL,
	external_id varchar NULL,
	namespace_name varchar NULL,
	job_name varchar NULL,
	"location" varchar NULL,
	transitioned_at timestamp NULL,
	started_at timestamp NULL,
	ended_at timestamp NULL,
	job_context_uuid uuid NULL,
	parent_run_uuid uuid NULL,
	job_uuid uuid NULL,
	CONSTRAINT runs_pkey PRIMARY KEY (uuid)
);
CREATE INDEX runs_created_at_by_name_index ON public.runs USING btree (job_name, namespace_name, created_at DESC) INCLUDE (uuid, created_at, updated_at, nominal_start_time, nominal_end_time, current_run_state, started_at, ended_at, namespace_name, job_name, location);
CREATE INDEX runs_created_at_completed_by_name_index ON public.runs USING btree (job_name, namespace_name, created_at DESC) INCLUDE (started_at, ended_at) WHERE ((current_run_state)::text = 'COMPLETED'::text);
CREATE INDEX runs_created_at_completed_index ON public.runs USING btree (created_at DESC) INCLUDE (job_name, namespace_name, started_at, ended_at) WHERE ((current_run_state)::text = 'COMPLETED'::text);
CREATE INDEX runs_created_at_current_run_state_index ON public.runs USING btree (created_at DESC, current_run_state);
CREATE INDEX runs_created_at_index ON public.runs USING btree (created_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX runs_end_run_state_uuid_index ON public.runs USING btree (end_run_state_uuid);
CREATE INDEX runs_job_uuid ON public.runs USING btree (job_uuid, transitioned_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX runs_parent_run_uuid_index ON public.runs USING btree (parent_run_uuid);
CREATE INDEX runs_start_run_state_uuid_index ON public.runs USING btree (start_run_state_uuid);

-- Table Triggers

create trigger runs_insert_job_uuid before
insert
    on
    public.runs for each row
    when (((new.job_uuid is null)
        and (new.job_name is not null)
            and (new.namespace_name is not null))) execute function write_run_job_uuid();

-- Permissions

ALTER TABLE runs OWNER TO marquez;
GRANT ALL ON TABLE runs TO marquez;


-- public.runs_input_mapping definition

-- Drop table

-- DROP TABLE runs_input_mapping;

CREATE TABLE runs_input_mapping (
	run_uuid uuid NOT NULL,
	dataset_version_uuid uuid NOT NULL,
	CONSTRAINT runs_input_mapping_pkey PRIMARY KEY (run_uuid, dataset_version_uuid)
);

-- Permissions

ALTER TABLE runs_input_mapping OWNER TO marquez;
GRANT ALL ON TABLE runs_input_mapping TO marquez;


-- public.dataset_facets foreign keys

ALTER TABLE public.dataset_facets ADD CONSTRAINT dataset_facets_dataset_uuid_fkey FOREIGN KEY (dataset_uuid) REFERENCES datasets("uuid") ON DELETE CASCADE;
ALTER TABLE public.dataset_facets ADD CONSTRAINT dataset_facets_dataset_version_uuid_fkey FOREIGN KEY (dataset_version_uuid) REFERENCES dataset_versions("uuid") ON DELETE CASCADE;
ALTER TABLE public.dataset_facets ADD CONSTRAINT dataset_facets_run_uuid_fkey FOREIGN KEY (run_uuid) REFERENCES runs("uuid") ON DELETE CASCADE;


-- public.run_facets foreign keys

ALTER TABLE public.run_facets ADD CONSTRAINT run_facets_run_uuid_fkey FOREIGN KEY (run_uuid) REFERENCES runs("uuid") ON DELETE CASCADE;


-- public.run_states foreign keys

ALTER TABLE public.run_states ADD CONSTRAINT run_states_run_uuid_fkey FOREIGN KEY (run_uuid) REFERENCES runs("uuid") ON DELETE CASCADE;


-- public.runs foreign keys

ALTER TABLE public.runs ADD CONSTRAINT runs_end_run_state_uuid_fkey FOREIGN KEY (end_run_state_uuid) REFERENCES run_states("uuid") ON DELETE CASCADE;
ALTER TABLE public.runs ADD CONSTRAINT runs_job_version_uuid_fkey FOREIGN KEY (job_version_uuid) REFERENCES job_versions("uuid") ON DELETE CASCADE;
ALTER TABLE public.runs ADD CONSTRAINT runs_parent_fk_runs FOREIGN KEY (parent_run_uuid) REFERENCES runs("uuid") ON DELETE CASCADE;
ALTER TABLE public.runs ADD CONSTRAINT runs_run_args_uuid_fkey FOREIGN KEY (run_args_uuid) REFERENCES run_args("uuid") ON DELETE CASCADE;
ALTER TABLE public.runs ADD CONSTRAINT runs_start_run_state_uuid_fkey FOREIGN KEY (start_run_state_uuid) REFERENCES run_states("uuid") ON DELETE CASCADE;


-- public.runs_input_mapping foreign keys

ALTER TABLE public.runs_input_mapping ADD CONSTRAINT runs_input_mapping_dataset_version_uuid_fkey FOREIGN KEY (dataset_version_uuid) REFERENCES dataset_versions("uuid") ON DELETE CASCADE;
ALTER TABLE public.runs_input_mapping ADD CONSTRAINT runs_input_mapping_run_uuid_fkey FOREIGN KEY (run_uuid) REFERENCES runs("uuid") ON DELETE CASCADE;
